SENTIENT SPECIES:
Purple Koboldoids with Five-fold Symmetry: Eat pretty much anything, including one another. Disturbingly fond of skulls. They have purple skin. They have five-fold symmetry. They are reclusive and have a complex system of social rules. They first evolved on Hylon II in 1210.
	Their Stats are: STR: 2 DEX: 0 CON: 2 INT: -1 CHA: -1
Feathered Yellow Robots: Purely mechanical lifeforms, artificially created. They have yellow feathers. They have bilateral symmetry. They are thrill-seeking and believe in the inherent superiority of their species. They were created by the Republic of Humanoids and Robots on Donet VI as servants in 1060.
	Their Stats are: STR: -1 DEX: 1 CON: 1 INT: 1 CHA: 1

CIVILISATIONS:
THE THIRD CHURCH OF GIANT HUMANOIDS WITH GIANT EYES:
An ancient, corrupt, fantastically wealthy, highly advanced Church of 19 planets, with 25 billion inhabitants.
Major populations:
5 billion enslaved Purple Koboldoids with Five-fold Symmetry.
20 billion enslaved Feathered Yellow Robots.

	Their Stats are: STR: 2 DEX: 0 CON: 0 INT: 0 CHA: 2
PLANETS:
MYCON II
A barren planet of the Third Church of Giant Humanoids with Giant Eyes.
A military base, built by the Third Church of Giant Humanoids with Giant Eyes in 1200
Periodical Darkness: Every thirteen years, the orbit of this planet synchronizes with that of a planet closer to its stars, causing a night that lasts for weeks.
Strata:
The ruins of a mining base, built by the Third Church of Giant Humanoids with Giant Eyes in 1124, destroyed in 594 by a time vortex.

It is populated by:
4 billion enslaved Feathered Yellow Robots
A science lab, built by the Third Church of Giant Humanoids with Giant Eyes in 1186
Deep Impenetrable Seas: Hundreds of kilometres down, water turns into ice from pressure.
Lifeforms of note:
Brain parasites: A parasitical creature able to interface with the brain of its host, enslaving it.
Ocean giants: Huge sea creatures growing to more than a kilometre of length.
Beautiful flying creatures: Fluttering fliers that display a dazzling array of colours.

The rogue AI Experiment 123 encases Asimov Cairn, Autarch of the Second Church of Giant Humanoids with Giant Eyes, in a block of time ice.
1223:
The population of Purple Koboldoids with Five-fold Symmetry on Cinax III has grown by a billion.
The population of Feathered Yellow Robots on Sativex III has grown by a billion.
Religious fanatics sieze power in the Second Church of Giant Humanoids with Giant Eyes and declare the Third Church of Giant Humanoids with Giant Eyes.
The rogue AI Experiment 123 vanishes without a trace.
